<h3 class="kt-adv-heading2103_7028bb-d8 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-1-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading2103_7028bb-d8">Meet the &#8220;She&#8221; Behind She Knows SEO</h3>



<h2 class="kt-adv-heading2103_31ef68-72 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading2103_31ef68-72">Hey, I&#8217;m Nina!</h2>



<p>Nina Clapperton is the founder of She Knows SEO. She has worked as a niche blogger since 2018, grew her travel blog to 50k sessions in 6 months, and now runs a portfolio of niche sites. </p>



<p>And in 2023, she hit over 250k pageviews and had her first $110k month!</p>



<p>She has helped over 7,500 students and clients with their blogs since starting She Knows SEO.</p>



<p>She&#8217;s on a mission to help bloggers achieve financial freedom via passive income from their blogs.</p>
